                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Monday, July 7, 2014
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-8tjK5xuXcB0/U7rjAsbtzaI/AAAAAAAAD6A/WFrzIpGIhjE/s1600/Planet-of-the-Apes+kiss.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="9018104899950239962" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="5742606172186283957" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="5742606172186283957">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     COMMENTARY - Planet Of The Apes
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5742606172186283957" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-8tjK5xuXcB0/U7rjAsbtzaI/AAAAAAAAD6A/WFrzIpGIhjE/s1600/Planet-of-the-Apes+kiss.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" closure_lm_209366="null" height="325" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-8tjK5xuXcB0/U7rjAsbtzaI/AAAAAAAAD6A/WFrzIpGIhjE/s1600/Planet-of-the-Apes+kiss.jpg" width="400" wua="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div style="text-align: justify;">
                      You know the how this works. Aaron had Jim Dietz and myself on to discuss all things planet of the Apes. Of course the discussion couldn't be JUST that. We talk about the franchise and science fiction of the era Planet of the Apes came out as well. Its another dynamite commentary discussion and it really could have gone well on through Beneath easily (we go past the credits a bit too). We'll save that for another day. But, for this day, here's the the commentary for the original.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: justify;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: justify;">
                      Click the link to listen!
                      <br/>
                      <a href="http://www.thecodeiszeek.com/2014/07/out-now-commentary-planet-of-apes-1968.html" target="_blank">
                       http://www.thecodeiszeek.com/2014/07/out-now-commentary-planet-of-apes-1968.html
                      </a>
                      <br/>
                     </div>
